<h2 id="examples" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#examples"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Examples</h2>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="placeholder" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#placeholder"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Placeholder</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To customize the default pin input placeholder <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">○</code> for each input, pass the placeholder prop and set it to your desired
value.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="blur-on-complete" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#blur-on-complete"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Blur on Complete</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">By default, the last input maintains focus when filled, and we invoke the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onValueComplete</code> callback. To blur the last
input when the user completes the input, set the prop <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">blurOnComplete</code> to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">true</code>.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8nhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8nhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8nhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="otp-mode" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#otp-mode"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>OTP Mode</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To trigger smartphone OTP auto-suggestion, it is recommended to set the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">autocomplete</code> attribute to &quot;one-time-code&quot;. The
pin input component provides support for this automatically when you set the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">otp</code> prop to true.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8thanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8thanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8thanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="masking" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#masking"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Masking</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">When collecting private or sensitive information using the pin input, you might need to mask the value entered, similar
to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">&lt;input type=&quot;password&quot;/&gt;</code>. Pass the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">mask</code> prop to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">true</code>.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_93hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_93hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_93hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="change-events" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#change-events"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Change Events</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The pin input component invokes several callback functions when the user enters:</p>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onValueChange</code> — Callback invoked when the value is changed.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onValueComplete</code> — Callback invoked when all fields have been completed (by typing or pasting).</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onValueInvalid</code> — Callback invoked when an invalid value is entered into the input. An invalid value is any value
that doesn&#x27;t match the specified &quot;type&quot;.</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="field" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#field"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Field</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Field</code> component helps manage form-related state and accessibility attributes of a pin input. It includes handling
ARIA labels, helper text, and error text to ensure proper accessibility.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9fhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9fhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9fhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="root-provider" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#root-provider"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Root Provider</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">An alternative way to control the pin input is to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RootProvider</code> component and the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">usePinInput</code> hook. This way
you can access the state and methods from outside the component.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9lhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9lhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9lhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h2 id="api-reference" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#api-reference"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>API Reference</h2>
<h3 id="props" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#props"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Props</h3>

<h2 id="accessibility" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#accessibility"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Accessibility</h2>
<h3 id="keyboard-support" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#keyboard-support"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Keyboard Support</h3>
<div class="bd-w_1px bdr_lg ov-x_auto not-prose"><table class="bd_0 table__root table__root--size_sm table__root--variant_outline"><thead class="table__head table__head--size_sm Anatomy\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"pin-input\" /\u003e\n\n```tsx\n\u003cPinInput.Root\u003e\n  \u003cPinInput.Label /\u003e\n  \u003cPinInput.Control\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.Input /\u003e\n  \u003c/PinInput.Control\u003e\n  \u003cPinInput.HiddenInput /\u003e\n\u003c/PinInput.Root\u003e\n```\n\n## Examples\n\n**Example: basic**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { PinInput } from '@ark-ui/react/pin-input'\nimport styles from 'styles/pin-input.module.css'\n\nexport const Basic = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cPinInput.Root className={styles.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.Label key={id} index={index} className={styles.Input} /\u003e\n      ))}\n    \u003c/PinInput.Control\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/PinInput.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { PinInput } from '@ark-ui/solid/pin-input'\nimport { Index } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/pin-input.module.css'\n\nexport const Basic = () =\u003e (\n \u003cIndex each={[0, 1, 2]}\u003e{(id) =\u003e \u003cPinInput.Input index={id()} class={styles.Input} /\u003e}\u003c/Index\u003e\n    \u003c/PinInput.Control\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/PinInput.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { PinInput } from '@ark-ui/vue/pin-input'\nimport styles from 'styles/pin-input.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cPinInput.Root :class=\"styles.Root\"\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.Label :index=\"id\" :class=\"styles.Input\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/PinInput.Control\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/PinInput.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { PinInput } from '@ark-ui/svelte/pin-input'\n  import styles from 'styles/pin-input.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cPinInput.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n  \u003cPinInput.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/PinInput.Label\u003e\n  \u003cPinInput.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n    {#each [0, 1, 2] as id, index (id)}\n      \u003cPinInput.Input {index} class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n    {/each}\n  \u003c/PinInput.Control\u003e\n  \u003cPinInput.HiddenInput /\u003e\n\u003c/PinInput.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Placeholder\n\nTo customize the default pin input placeholder `○` for each input, pass the placeholder prop and set it to your desired\nvalue.\n\n**Example: custom-placeholder**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { PinInput } from '@ark-ui/react/pin-input'\nimport styles from 'styles/pin-input.module.css'\n\nexport const CustomPlaceholder = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cPinInput.Root className={styles.Root} placeholder=\"*\"\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/PinInput.Label\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n      {[0, 1, 2].map((id, index) =\u003e (\n        \u003cPinInput.Input key={id} index={index} className={styles.Input} /\u003e\n      ))}\n    \u003c/PinInput.Control\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/PinInput.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { PinInput } from '@ark-ui/solid/pin-input'\nimport { Index } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/pin-input.module.css'\n\nexport const CustomPlaceholder = () =\u003e \u003cPinInput.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/PinInput.Label\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cPinInput.Input v-for=\"id in [0, 1, 2]\" input maintains focus when filled, and we invoke the `onValueComplete` callback. To blur the last\ninput when the user completes the input, set the prop `blurOnComplete` to `true`.\n\n**Example: blur-on-complete**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { PinInput } from '@ark-ui/react/pin-input'\nimport styles from 'styles/pin-input.module.css'\n\nexport const BlurOnComplete = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cPinInput.Root className={styles.Root} blurOnComplete\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/PinInput.Label\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n      {[0, 1, 2].map((id, index) =\u003e (\n        \u003cPinInput.Input key={id} index={index} className={styles.Input} /\u003e\n      ))}\n    \u003c/PinInput.Control\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/PinInput.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { PinInput } from '@ark-ui/solid/pin-input'\nimport { Index } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/pin-input.module.css'\n\nexport const BlurOnComplete = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cPinInput.Root class={styles.Root} blurOnComplete\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/PinInput.Label\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cIndex each={[0, 1, 2]}\u003e{(id) =\u003e \u003cPinInput.Input index={id()} class={styles.Input} /\u003e}\u003c/Index\u003e\n    \u003c/PinInput.Control\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/PinInput.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { PinInput } from '@ark-ui/vue/pin-input'\nimport styles from 'styles/pin-input.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cPinInput.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" blurOnComplete\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/PinInput.Label\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cPinInput.Input v-for=\"id in [0, 1, 2]\" :key=\"id\" :index=\"id\" :class=\"styles.Input\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/PinInput.Control\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/PinInput.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { PinInput } from class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/PinInput.Label\u003e\n  \u003cPinInput.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n    {#each [0, 1, 2] as id, index (id)}\n      \u003cPinInput.Input {index} class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n    {/each}\n  \u003c/PinInput.Control\u003e\n  \u003cPinInput.HiddenInput /\u003e\n\u003c/PinInput.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### OTP Mode\n\nTo trigger smartphone OTP auto-suggestion, it is recommended to set the `autocomplete` attribute to \"one-time-code\". The\npin input component provides support for this automatically when you set the `otp` prop to true.\n\n**Example: otp-mode**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { PinInput } from '@ark-ui/react/pin-input'\nimport styles from 'styles/pin-input.module.css'\n\nexport const OTPMode = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cPinInput.Root className={styles.Root} otp\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/PinInput.Label\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n      {[0, 1, 2].map((id, index) =\u003e (\n        \u003cPinInput.Input key={id} index={index} className={styles.Input} /\u003e\n      ))}\n    \u003c/PinInput.Control\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/PinInput.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { PinInput } from '@ark-ui/solid/pin-input'\nimport { Index } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/pin-input.module.css'\n\nexport const OTPMode = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cPinInput.Root class={styles.Root} otp\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/PinInput.Label\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cIndex each={[0, 1, 2]}\u003e{(id) =\u003e \u003cPinInput.Input index={id()} class={styles.Input} /\u003e}\u003c/Index\u003e\n    \u003c/PinInput.Control\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/PinInput.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { PinInput } from '@ark-ui/vue/pin-input'\nimport styles from 'styles/pin-input.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cPinInput.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" otp\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/PinInput.Label\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cPinInput.Input v-for=\"id in [0, 1, 2]\" :key=\"id\" :index=\"id\" :class=\"styles.Input\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/PinInput.Control\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/PinInput.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### 'styles/pin-input.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cPinInput.Root class={styles.Root} otp\u003e\n  \u003cPinInput.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/PinInput.Label\u003e\n  \u003cPinInput.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n    {#each [0, 1, 2] as id, index (id)}\n      \u003cPinInput.Input {index} class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n    {/each}\n  \u003c/PinInput.Control\u003e\n  \u003cPinInput.HiddenInput /\u003e\n\u003c/PinInput.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Masking\n\nWhen collecting private or sensitive information using the pin input, you might need to mask the value entered, similar\nto `\u003cinput type=\"password\"/\u003e`. Pass the `mask` prop to `true`.\n\n**Example: mask**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { PinInput } from '@ark-ui/react/pin-input'\nimport styles from 'styles/pin-input.module.css'\n\nexport const Mask = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cPinInput.Root className={styles.Root} mask\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/PinInput.Label\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n      {[0, 1, 2].map((id, index) =\u003e (\n        \u003cPinInput.Input key={id} index={index} className={styles.Input} /\u003e\n      ))}\n    \u003c/PinInput.Control\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/PinInput.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { PinInput } from '@ark-ui/solid/pin-input'\nimport { Index } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/pin-input.module.css'\n\nexport const Mask = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cPinInput.Root class={styles.Root} mask\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/PinInput.Label\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cIndex each={[0, 1, 2]}\u003e{(id) =\u003e \u003cPinInput.Input index={id()} class={styles.Input} /\u003e}\u003c/Index\u003e\n    \u003c/PinInput.Control\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/PinInput.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { PinInput } from '@ark-ui/vue/pin-input'\nimport styles from 'styles/pin-input.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cPinInput.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" mask\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/PinInput.Label\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cPinInput.Input v-for=\"id in [0, 1, 2]\" :key=\"id\" :index=\"id\" :class=\"styles.Input\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/PinInput.Control\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/PinInput.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { PinInput } from '@ark-ui/svelte/pin-input'\n  import styles from 'styles/pin-input.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cPinInput.Root class={styles.Root} mask\u003e\n  \u003cPinInput.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/PinInput.Label\u003e\n  \u003cPinInput.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n    {#each [0, 1, 2] as id, index (id)}\n      \u003cPinInput.Input {index} class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n    {/each}\n  \u003c/PinInput.Control\u003e\n  \u003cPinInput.HiddenInput /\u003e\n\u003c/PinInput.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Change Events\n\nThe pin input component invokes several callback functions when the user enters:\n\n- `onValueChange` — Callback invoked when the value is changed.\n- `onValueComplete` — Callback invoked when all fields have been completed (by typing or pasting).\n- `onValueInvalid` — Callback invoked when an invalid value is entered into the input. An invalid value is any value\n  that doesn't match the specified \"type\".\n\n### Field\n\nThe `Field` component helps manage form-related state and accessibility attributes of a pin input. It includes handling\nARIA labels, helper text, and error text to ensure proper accessibility.\n\n**Example: with-field**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Field } from '@ark-ui/react/field'\nimport { PinInput } from '@ark-ui/react/pin-input'\nimport fieldStyles from 'styles/field.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/pin-input.module.css'\n\nexport const WithField = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cField.Root className={fieldStyles.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.Root className={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cPinInput.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/PinInput.Label\u003e\n      \u003cPinInput.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        {[0, 1, 2].map((id, index) =\u003e (\n          \u003cPinInput.Input key={id} index={index} className={styles.Input} /\u003e\n        ))}\n      \u003c/PinInput.Control\u003e\n      \u003cPinInput.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/PinInput.Root\u003e\n    \u003cField.HelperText className={fieldStyles.HelperText}\u003eAdditional Info\u003c/Field.HelperText\u003e\n    \u003cField.ErrorText className={fieldStyles.ErrorText}\u003eError Info\u003c/Field.ErrorText\u003e\n  \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Field } from '@ark-ui/solid/field'\nimport { PinInput } from '@ark-ui/solid/pin-input'\nimport { Index } from 'solid-js'\nimport fieldStyles from 'styles/field.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/pin-input.module.css'\n\nexport const WithField = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cField.Root class={fieldStyles.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cPinInput.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/PinInput.Label\u003e\n      \u003cPinInput.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cIndex each={[0, 1, 2]}\u003e{(id) =\u003e \u003cPinInput.Input index={id()} class={styles.Input} /\u003e}\u003c/Index\u003e\n      \u003c/PinInput.Control\u003e\n      \u003cPinInput.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/PinInput.Root\u003e\n    \u003cField.HelperText class={fieldStyles.HelperText}\u003eAdditional Info\u003c/Field.HelperText\u003e\n    \u003cField.ErrorText class={fieldStyles.ErrorText}\u003eError Info\u003c/Field.ErrorText\u003e\n  \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Field } from '@ark-ui/vue/field'\nimport { PinInput } from '@ark-ui/vue/pin-input'\nimport fieldStyles from 'styles/field.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/pin-input.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cField.Root :class=\"fieldStyles.Root\"\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.Root :class=\"styles.Root\"\u003e\n      \u003cPinInput.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/PinInput.Label\u003e\n      \u003cPinInput.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n        \u003cPinInput.Input v-for=\"id in [0, 1, 2]\" :key=\"id\" :index=\"id\" :class=\"styles.Input\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/PinInput.Control\u003e\n      \u003cPinInput.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/PinInput.Root\u003e\n    \u003cField.HelperText :class=\"fieldStyles.HelperText\"\u003eAdditional Info\u003c/Field.HelperText\u003e\n    \u003cField.ErrorText :class=\"fieldStyles.ErrorText\"\u003eError Info\u003c/Field.ErrorText\u003e\n  \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Field } from '@ark-ui/svelte/field'\n  import { PinInput } from '@ark-ui/svelte/pin-input'\n  import fieldStyles from 'styles/field.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/pin-input.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cField.Root class={fieldStyles.Root}\u003e\n  \u003cPinInput.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/PinInput.Label\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n      {#each [0, 1, 2] as id, index (id)}\n        \u003cPinInput.Input {index} class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n      {/each}\n    \u003c/PinInput.Control\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/PinInput.Root\u003e\n  \u003cField.HelperText class={fieldStyles.HelperText}\u003eAdditional Info\u003c/Field.HelperText\u003e\n  \u003cField.ErrorText class={fieldStyles.ErrorText}\u003eError Info\u003c/Field.ErrorText\u003e\n\u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Root Provider\n\nAn alternative way to control the pin input is to use the `RootProvider` component and the `usePinInput` hook. This way\nyou can access the state and methods from outside the component.\n\n**Example: root-provider**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { PinInput, usePinInput } from '@ark-ui/react/pin-input'\nimport styles from 'styles/pin-input.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const pinInput = usePinInput({ onValueComplete: (e) =\u003e alert(e.valueAsString) })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003cbutton onClick={() =\u003e pinInput.focus()}\u003eFocus\u003c/button\u003e\n\n      \u003cPinInput.RootProvider value={pinInput} className={styles.Root}\u003e\n        \u003cPinInput.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/PinInput.Label\u003e\n        \u003cPinInput.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n          {[0, 1, 2].map((id, index) =\u003e (\n            \u003cPinInput.Input key={id} index={index} className={styles.Input} /\u003e\n          ))}\n        \u003c/PinInput.Control\u003e\n        \u003cPinInput.HiddenInput /\u003e\n      \u003c/PinInput.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { PinInput, usePinInput } from '@ark-ui/solid/pin-input'\nimport { Index } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/pin-input.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const pinInput = usePinInput({ onValueComplete: (e) =\u003e alert(e.valueAsString) })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003cbutton onClick={() =\u003e pinInput().focus()}\u003eFocus\u003c/button\u003e\n\n      \u003cPinInput.RootProvider value={pinInput} class={styles.Root}\u003e\n        \u003cPinInput.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/PinInput.Label\u003e\n        \u003cPinInput.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n          \u003cIndex each={[0, 1, 2]}\u003e{(id) =\u003e \u003cPinInput.Input index={id()} class={styles.Input} /\u003e}\u003c/Index\u003e\n        \u003c/PinInput.Control\u003e\n        \u003cPinInput.HiddenInput /\u003e\n      \u003c/PinInput.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { PinInput, usePinInput } from '@ark-ui/vue/pin-input'\nimport styles from 'styles/pin-input.module.css'\n\nconst pinInput = usePinInput()\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n    \u003cbutton @click=\"pinInput.focus()\"\u003eFocus\u003c/button\u003e\n\n    \u003cPinInput.RootProvider :value=\"pinInput\" :class=\"styles.Root\"\u003e\n      \u003cPinInput.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/PinInput.Label\u003e\n      \u003cPinInput.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n        \u003cPinInput.Input v-for=\"id in [0, 1, 2]\" :key=\"id\" :index=\"id\" :class=\"styles.Input\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/PinInput.Control\u003e\n      \u003cPinInput.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/PinInput.RootProvider\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { PinInput, usePinInput } from '@ark-ui/svelte/pin-input'\n  import styles from 'styles/pin-input.module.css'\n\n  const id = $props.id()\n\n  const pinInput = usePinInput({ id, onValueComplete: (e) =\u003e alert(e.valueAsString) })\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n  \u003cbutton onclick={() =\u003e pinInput().focus()}\u003eFocus\u003c/button\u003e\n\n  \u003cPinInput.RootProvider value={pinInput} class={styles.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/PinInput.Label\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n      {#each [0, 1, 2] as id, index (id)}\n        \u003cPinInput.Input {index} class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n      {/each}\n    \u003c/PinInput.Control\u003e\n    \u003cPinInput.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/PinInput.RootProvider\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n## API Reference\n\n### Props\n\n**Component API Reference**\n\n#### React\n\n**Root Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n| `autoFocus` | `boolean` | No | Whether to auto-focus the first input. |\n| `blurOnComplete` | `boolean` | No | Whether to blur the input when the value is complete |\n| `count` | `number` | No | The number of inputs to render to improve SSR aria attributes.\nThis will be required in next major version. |\n| `defaultValue` | `string[]` | No | The initial value of the the pin input when rendered.\nUse when you don't need to control the value of the pin input. |\n| `disabled` | `boolean` | No | Whether the inputs are disabled |\n| `form` | `string` | No | The associate form of the underlying input element. |\n| `id` | `string` | No | The unique identifier of the machine. |\n| `ids` | `Partial\u003c{\n  root: string\n  hiddenInput: string\n  label: string\n  control: string\n  input: (id: string) =\u003e string\n}\u003e` | No | The ids of the elements in the pin input. Useful for composition. |\n| `invalid` | `boolean` | No | Whether the pin input is in the invalid state |\n| `mask` | `boolean` | No | If `true`, the input's value will be masked just like `type=password` |\n| `name` | `string` | No | The name of the input element. Useful for form submission. |\n| `onValueChange` | `(details: ValueChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Function called on input change |\n| `onValueComplete` | `(details: ValueChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Function called when all inputs have valid values |\n| `onValueInvalid` | `(details: ValueInvalidDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Function called when an invalid value is entered |\n| `otp` | `boolean` | No | If `true`, the pin input component signals to its fields that they should\nuse `autocomplete=\"one-time-code\"`. |\n| `pattern` | `string` | No | The regular expression that the user-entered input value is checked against. |\n| `placeholder` | `string` | No | The placeholder text for the input |\n| `readOnly` | `boolean` | No | Whether the pin input is in the valid state |\n| `required` | `boolean` | No | Whether the pin input is required |\n| `selectOnFocus` | `boolean` | No | Whether to select input value when input is focused |\n| `translations` | `IntlTranslations` | No | Specifies the localized strings that identifies the accessibility elements and their states |\n| `type` | `'numeric' | 'alphanumeric' | 'alphabetic'` | No | The type of value the pin-input should allow |\n| `value` | `string[]` | No | The controlled value of the the pin input. |\n\n\n**Root Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | pin-input |\n| `[data-part]` | root |\n| `[data-invalid]` | Present when invalid |\n| `[data-disabled]` | Present when disabled |\n| `[data-complete]` | Present when the pin-input value is complete |\n| `[data-readonly]` | Present when read-only |\n\n\n**Control Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**HiddenInput Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Input Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `index` | `number` | Yes |  |\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Input Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | pin-input |\n| `[data-part]` | input |\n| `[data-disabled]` | Present when disabled |\n| `[data-complete]` | Present when the input value is complete |\n| `[data-index]` | The index of the item |\n| `[data-invalid]` | Present when invalid |\n\n\n**Label Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Label Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | pin-input |\n| `[data-part]` | label |\n| `[data-invalid]` | Present when invalid |\n| `[data-disabled]` | Present when disabled |\n| `[data-complete]` | Present when the label value is complete |\n| `[data-required]` | Present when required |\n| `[data-readonly]` | Present when read-only |\n\n\n**RootProvider Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `value` | `UsePinInputReturn` | Yes |  |\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n#### Solid\n\n**Root Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `(props: ParentProps\u003c'div'\u003e) =\u003e Element` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n| `autoFocus` | `boolean` | No | Whether to auto-focus the first input. |\n| `blurOnComplete` | `boolean` | No | Whether to blur the input when the value is complete |\n| `count` | `number` | No | The number of inputs to render to improve SSR aria attributes.\nThis will be required in next major version. |\n| `defaultValue` | `string[]` | No | The initial value of the the pin input when rendered.\nUse when you don't need to control the value of the pin input. |\n| `disabled` | `boolean` | No | Whether the inputs are disabled |\n| `form` | `string` | No | The associate form of the underlying input element. |\n| `ids` | `Partial\u003c{\n  root: string\n  hiddenInput: string\n  label: string\n  control: string\n  input: (id: string) =\u003e string\n}\u003e` | No | The ids of the elements in the pin input. Useful for composition. |\n| `invalid` | `boolean` | No | Whether the pin input is in the invalid state |\n| `mask` | `boolean` | No | If `true`, the input's value will be masked just like `type=password` |\n| `name` | `string` | No | The name of the input element. Useful for form submission. |\n| `onValueChange` | `(details: ValueChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Function called on input change |\n| `onValueComplete` | `(details: ValueChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Function called when all inputs have valid values |\n| `onValueInvalid` | `(details: ValueInvalidDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Function called when an invalid value is entered |\n| `otp` | `boolean` | No | If `true`, the pin input component signals to its fields that they should\nuse `autocomplete=\"one-time-code\"`. |\n| `pattern` | `string` | No | The regular expression that the user-entered input value is checked against. |\n| `placeholder` | `string` | No | The placeholder text for the input |\n| `readOnly` | `boolean` | No | Whether the pin input is in the valid state |\n| `required` | `boolean` | No | Whether the pin input is required |\n| `selectOnFocus` | `boolean` | No | Whether to select input value when input is focused |\n| `translations` | `IntlTranslations` | No | Specifies the localized strings that identifies the accessibility elements and their states |\n| `type` | `'numeric' | 'alphanumeric' | 'alphabetic'` | No | The type of value the pin-input should allow |\n| `value` | `string[]` | No | The controlled value of the the pin input. |\n\n\n**Root Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | pin-input |\n| `[data-part]` | root |\n| `[data-invalid]` | Present when invalid |\n| `[data-disabled]` | Present when disabled |\n| `[data-complete]` | Present when the pin-input value is complete |\n| `[data-readonly]` | Present when read-only |\n\n\n**Control Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `(props: ParentProps\u003c'div'\u003e) =\u003e Element` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**HiddenInput Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `(props: ParentProps\u003c'input'\u003e) =\u003e Element` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Input Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `index` | `number` | Yes |  |\n| `asChild` | `(props: ParentProps\u003c'input'\u003e) =\u003e Element` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Input Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | pin-input |\n| `[data-part]` | input |\n| `[data-disabled]` | Present when disabled |\n| `[data-complete]` | Present when the input value is complete |\n| `[data-index]` | The index of the item |\n| `[data-invalid]` | Present when invalid |\n\n\n**Label Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `(props: ParentProps\u003c'label'\u003e) =\u003e Element` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Label Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | pin-input |\n| `[data-part]` | label |\n| `[data-invalid]` | Present when invalid |\n| `[data-disabled]` | Present when disabled |\n| `[data-complete]` | Present when the label value is complete |\n| `[data-required]` | Present when required |\n| `[data-readonly]` | Present when read-only |\n\n\n**RootProvider Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `value` | `UsePinInputReturn` | Yes |  |\n| `asChild` | `(props: ParentProps\u003c'div'\u003e) =\u003e Element` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n#### Vue\n\n**Root Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n| `autoFocus` | `boolean` | No | Whether to auto-focus the first input. |\n| `blurOnComplete` | `boolean` | No | Whether to blur the input when the value is complete |\n| `count` | `number` | No | The number of inputs to render to improve SSR aria attributes.\nThis will be required in next major version. |\n| `defaultValue` | `string[]` | No | The initial value of the the pin input when rendered.\nUse when you don't need to control the value of the pin input. |\n| `disabled` | `boolean` | No | Whether the inputs are disabled |\n| `form` | `string` | No | The associate form of the underlying input element. |\n| `id` | `string` | No | The unique identifier of the machine. |\n| `ids` | `Partial\u003c{\n  root: string\n  hiddenInput: string\n  label: string\n  control: string\n  input(id: string): string\n}\u003e` | No | The ids of the elements in the pin input. Useful for composition. |\n| `invalid` | `boolean` | No | Whether the pin input is in the invalid state |\n| `mask` | `boolean` | No | If `true`, the input's value will be masked just like `type=password` |\n| `modelValue` | `string[]` | No | The v-model value of the pin input |\n| `name` | `string` | No | The name of the input element. Useful for form submission. |\n| `otp` | `boolean` | No | If `true`, the pin input component signals to its fields that they should\nuse `autocomplete=\"one-time-code\"`. |\n| `pattern` | `string` | No | The regular expression that the user-entered input value is checked against. |\n| `placeholder` | `string` | No | The placeholder text for the input |\n| `readOnly` | `boolean` | No | Whether the
